This is a well lit, large market with a halal butcher, restaurant and jewelry vendor. The grocery isles are well stocked with dry goods such as beans, grains, spices, products from the Middle East and North Africa, milk, yoghurt, cheese, freshly made bread, candy, including halal gummy bears, household items, including Islamic home decor. <username>Deirdre McGaffey Schwein</username><Date>1509664899888</Date><Rate>5</Rate>< Text>
I had found at a yard sale from my parents' condo a box of really nice blue and grey/silver tiles. We fell in love with them, so we decided to use their color to finish the bathroom. That was harder than you might think. After many unsuccessful and frustrating trips to Home Depot, I was convinced to go to Sherman Williams. I hit their store at 6 o'clock the next morning, and explained to the gentleman there that not only was I trying to match this really hard color, but if possible I needed the paint today, since the parents were coming to visit that weekend, and we were hoping to have it all done.

The people there were fantastic. Not only were they able to match the blue perfectly, they got it done in just a few hours. I have no idea what goes into paint matching, but to give you an idea - the tiles were most definitely blue, except when you put them next to paint chips, the ones that matched were purple. The paint the ended up mixing for us is actually designed for automotive work, it's purple when the light is directly on it, or when the paint is thin, but other than that it is the most amazing deep blue you've seen in a while.</Text>

Not sure what to call this place but a golf course is not appropriate. The greens resemble the landscape of moon with deep craters that make your ball bounce all directions. The carts have so so little charge they have to be pushed up hills which is dangerous and annonying. The coup de gras was the pin stuck in fairway of hole 12, the green was so bad they shoved the flag into an arbitrary area making the hole the wrong distance and unplayable. Speaking of distance, good luck finding a marker..you will find yourself guessing distance on nearly every shot.
We were terrified crossing the bridges on this course for fear of death and dismemberment. If you are hurt clearly there isn't enough money to cover your injuries. God forbid you might even become the owner!

Play at your own risk...<//review>

<user>102436351333453980546<//user>< name>
Stacy Langel< /name>
< date>
1598489396311< /date>
<Rate>2< /Rate>< Review>
Normally, I'm a fan of Black Angus, especially for their prime rib dinners. Tonight was the first time I placed an order to go. I ordered the prime rib & mud pie. Now, portion wise, the serving size was satisfactory. I got the 8oz, medium-well. My sides were the steak soup, which is another favorite. The prime rib, for some reason, is much better when served on a platter in the dining room. It lacked that savory flavor, which may have been a result of the 20 minute car ride home. Another disappointment was the bread loaf, which again, I normally love! It didn't survive the drive home. By the time I went to unwrap it, it was rock hard; and I do mean, rock hard.

*the takeaway for me is, if you can avoid take out and have the time to dine it, it's worth it. Prime rib to go, was just not worth the $50 price tag.

I also have a slight concern. After placing my order at the bar, I also ordered 2 drinks..and the tender did not change his gloves. The same gloves used to handle card, cash, pens, and receipts.. were used to pour and hand me 2 drinks. I dont understand the purpose of the gloves, if not just to protect the person serving the food, because they did nothing to protect me from the germs on everything handled before my drinks were made.</Review>

< review>
Great steak and grills restaurant in Whittier, CA, with fair price, and great services.  My wife loves to eat steaks here, almost the only steak restaurant in the area that we would go to. Try to join the club, so you would receive coupons on emails frequently.  Try their caesar salad and a side order of green beans with bacon bites, the best in the area.  Also, during lunch on Monday to Saturday, try the high noon lunch entrees.  For $15 to $19, you could have a variety of choice.  My wife often orders New York steak high noon lunch entree and my kids would like prime ribs, it comes with 2 sides, a beverage, and 2 pieces of chocolate cookies.</review>

<rate>1</rate><Text>I must compliment some consistency with food quality and service (4 stars).

The management brings it all down to one star:  (1) They are too lazy to "table touch" - thank a customer for coming or ask how the food is, (2) Likewise managers are too lazy to pitch-in to help when an unexpected surge of customer traffic occurs, slowing-down service, and (3) I purchased a $150 gift card that did not work for the family I gave it to.  I wrote the disappointed family a $150 check when they returned home, and it took me 3 trips (45 miles), with my $150 purchase receipt in-hand, for management to figure out what happened. <user_id>104816559186060466898<//user_id><rating>5</rating>< Text>
The good news: The food quality is superb! I find it hard to criticize the food here as it is nothing less than great. The molasses bread starter. Delightful! The spinach and artichoke dip appetizer. Delicious! And that Big Mountain Fudge Cake... whatever it's called. Slap-your-mama good! The parking here, thanks in no small part to the spacious outdoor mall area, is hassle-free even on busy nights. The staff did their job and always with a smile.

The bad news: It can get fairly packed here, but honestly, that speaks more to the restaurant's quality and likely people's desire for a solid dining experience. That said, there have been cases of patron abandonment or wait staff forgetfulness.

My suggestion: Give it a try if you like steaks or are looking for something with a little more substance than Applebee's or Denny's.< /Text>

I would call this a more commercialized restaurant like a sizzlers.

Service was about a 2 stars! I don't think a saw one server over the age of 18 except the bartender and one manager that walked the floor. Usually restaurant managers walk the floor to talk to their guest, not this one.

Food was not the best, the prime rib was not grill marked property. Now most commercialized business use a oven burner grill with metal grates so you can't mess up the marks. Not here, the steak was suppose to be Med-rare. What I got was rare on half and med rare on the other half. That would suggest half the grill of or a line cook and kitchen manager that's not checking or doesn't care. Last line of defence was the server, but at her age I doubt she could tell the difference.

Sorry guys, you have some real work to do!< /Review>

< review>
Server was attentive without being intrusive, all while keeping bar in addition.

We both had the Quick Cut lunch. 1/2 French dip beef with French fries, plus one side order.

She had the potato soup, which she praised and nommed. I ordered the Cesar salad, which I thought was great too...the dressing was fantastic, and so were the croutons ( which she kept stealing to dip in her soup ).

The sandwich was on a fresh half French roll and was piled high with thin sliced beef. The a jus was concentrated beefy flavor. Loved it. Half a sandwich was plenty. And the price was just under 10 bucks each.

Good service, good food, good value. 5 stars.<//review>
